NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICES
Notice is hereby given to the public that the Company M/s. DEKOMTE MB FABRIC EXPANSION JOINTS LIMITED having
registered office at 3/136, East Coast Road, Vettuvankeni Village, Injambakkam, Chennai-600 041 has passed a Special
Resolution at the Extraordinary meeting held on 16th March 2009 for voluntarily liquidating the company as follows:—
“Resolved that pursuant to the provisions of Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, the consent of the members
of the Company, be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the Company as the members’ voluntary winding up,
with effect from 16th March 2009.”
The above said resolution and connected documents will be filed with the Registrar of Companies, Tamil Nadu, Chennai
in due course.
Chennai,
17th March 2009.

R. RAJAGOPAL,
Director.
